# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 02:38:23.336205

### Base Program

```py
def racecar(target: int) -> int:
    memo = {}
    def dp(position, speed):
        if abs(position) > 2 * target:
            return target + 1
        if position == target:
            return 0 if speed == 1 else 1
        if (position, speed) in memo:
            return memo[(position, speed)]
        
        ans = dp(position + speed // 2, -speed // 2) + 1 if speed > 0 else dp(position - speed // 2, -speed // 2) + 1
        ans = min(ans, dp(position + speed, speed * 2) + 1)
        memo[(position, speed)] = ans
        return ans
    
    return dp(0, 1)
```

### Input

```json
None
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def racecar(target: int) -> int:
    memo = {}

    def dp(position, speed):
        if abs(position) > 2 * target:
            return target + 1
        if position == target:
            return 0 if speed == 1 else 1
        if (position, speed) in memo:
            return memo[position, speed]
        ans = dp(position + speed // 2, -speed // 2) + 1 if speed > 0 else dp(position - speed // 2, -speed // 2) + 1
        ans = min(ans, dp(position + speed, speed * 2) + 1)
        memo[position, speed] = ans
        return ans
    return dp(0, 1)
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def racecar(var_0: int) -> int:
    memo = {}

    def dp(var_1, var_2):
        if abs(var_1) > 2 * target:
            return target + 1
        if var_1 == target:
            return 0 if var_2 == 1 else 1
        if (var_1, var_2) in memo:
            return memo[var_1, var_2]
        ans = dp(var_1 + var_2 // 2, -var_2 // 2) + 1 if var_2 > 0 else dp(var_1 - var_2 // 2, -var_2 // 2) + 1
        ans = min(ans, dp(var_1 + var_2, var_2 * 2) + 1)
        memo[var_1, var_2] = ans
        return ans
    return dp(0, 1)
```

</details>

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def racecar(target: int) -> int:
    memo = {}

    def dp(position, speed):
        if abs(position) > target * 2:
            return 1 + target
        if position == target:
            return 0 if speed == 1 else 1
        if (position, speed) in memo:
            return memo[position, speed]
        ans = 1 + dp(speed // 2 + position, -speed // 2) if speed > 0 else 1 + dp(position + -(speed // 2), -speed // 2)
        ans = min(ans, 1 + dp(speed + position, 2 * speed))
        memo[position, speed] = ans
        return ans
    return dp(0, 1)
```

<details>

```
Success
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def racecar(var_3: int) -> int:
    memo = {}

    def dp(var_4, var_5):
        if abs(var_4) > target * 2:
            return 1 + target
        if var_4 == target:
            return 0 if var_5 == 1 else 1
        if (var_4, var_5) in memo:
            return memo[var_4, var_5]
        ans = 1 + dp(var_5 // 2 + var_4, -var_5 // 2) if var_5 > 0 else 1 + dp(var_4 + -(var_5 // 2), -var_5 // 2)
        ans = min(ans, 1 + dp(var_5 + var_4, 2 * var_5))
        memo[var_4, var_5] = ans
        return ans
    return dp(0, 1)
```
